\doxysubsubsection{Detailed Description}
Include \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{vec__swizzle_8hpp}{glm/gtx/vec\+\_\+swizzle.\+hpp}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} to use the features of this extension.

Functions to perform swizzle operation.
